          <xbrli:measure>xbrli:shares</xbrli:measure>

      </xbrli:divide>
    </xbrli:unit>
    </ix:resources>
  </ix:header>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif"><b>Item
8.01. Other Events</b></span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">On
February 3, 2020, IBM notified The Bank of New York Mellon, as trustee, that it will redeem its $500 million aggregate
principal amount of 2.900% Notes due 2021, $1,500 million aggregate principal amount of 2.800% Notes due 2021 and $900
million aggregate principal amount 2.250% Notes due 2021, in each case in full at the applicable redemption price
calculated in accordance with the indenture governing the notes, plus accrued and unpaid interest. The redemption date for
the notes will be March 6, 2020. This Current Report on Form 8-K is not a notice of redemption.</span></p>
